<Name>Gabriella Berrios< /Name><Date>1621322167734</Date><rating>4<//rating>< text>
Came across this when googling Korean fried chicken places, and decided to give it a go.
Ordered the combo #1 and an order of Korean kimchi tacos.
The combo was hands down the winner. They give you the entire bird, your choice of flavoring, medium sweet potato pizza , and 2 liter soda of choice.
It wasn‚Äôt as crunchy as other Korean fried chicken that I‚Äôve had, but the flavor and juiciness  of the chicken made up for that. That and the freshness of the chicken too. The sweet garlic sauce won over the soy sauce option in my opinion.
The sweet potato pizza was surprisingly good. I‚Äôve never agreed with pineapple on pizza, but it worked well with the rest of the ingredients. The pizza bread was dense and soft, but not the type that leaves you in a bloated food coma like other pizza doughs.
The kimchi tacos where pretty disappointing, the tortillas weren‚Äôt toasted or warmed, and the added salsa and sour cream didn‚Äôt mesh well with the bulgogi and kimchi. I honestly didn‚Äôt even taste the kimchi in there.
Aside from the taco that was a huge disappointment, I‚Äôm going to go back to try other flavors that caught my eye.<//text>

< review>
Having been to the ice cream shop next door, we saw Pa-Dak and were curious. When we walked in, service was prompt and friendly, but the place was a tad messy, as if they had just experienced a big rush.

We didn't know what to expect from the chicken (which is the reason we came), but I suppose I was expecting something a bit unusual. Most of the other Korean cuisine I've tried has a distinct flavor profile, and maybe I was hoping for some distinctiveness in the fried chicken.

Well, it's fried chicken. It was hot, crisp, and good; but not distinctive. The batter is somewhat crunchier than our typical fried fare; which was interesting, but again, not distinctive.

I can't comment on the other dishes, but they get good reviews here, so perhaps I'll try again.</review>

This is the best, crispy KFC (Korean Fried Chicken) in the area.  Get the sweet spicy sauce on the side to preserve crispiness.  The side of pickled radish cuts the richness a bit. Pizza is interesting but only ok.

<Date>1557633693622<//Date><Rating>5< /Rating><text>Great plaxe for pizza!< /text><Pics>None< /Pics><Resp>None<//Resp><Gmap_id>0x80dd2d049ddc97ab:0x9b17451e6cbb14d< /Gmap_id></record></dataset><record>

<Review>Attack of the Flying Chicken Pa-Dak!!

When I say corn, you say cheese!  Corn!  Cheese!  Corn!  Cheese!

When I say foul, you say fart!  Foul!  Fart!  Foul!  Fart!

Flatulence is a small price to pay, for when corn cheese tantalizes the tastebuds.

Flying Chicken Pa-Dak, formerly Pizza & Chicken Love Letter, is a casual Korean restaurant serving pizza, chicken, chicken wings, popcorn chicken & small bites, along with beer (draft & bottled) & soju.  Beer towers, too!  Gracing my sexy presence by walking in, I already knew I wanted the corn cheese.

Complimentary salad greeted me as I waited for my order to be up.
A large heaping helping of shredded cabbage, corn & dressing, the salad was crisp, light & a great way to stay regular.  Considering the amount and it's complimentary, it was great!

Corn cheese ($5.99)
Corn, cheese & a few pineapple chunks.  Simple, yet effective.  Melted gooey, fatty, unctuous cheese was incredibly delectable.  Corn niblets, a lot of them, provided the sweetness & the brightness came from the pineapple chunks.  I normally prefer pineapple fresh by itself, but I'm glad Flying Chicken Pa-Dak didn't go overboard with it, as the pina went well with the dish.  Anymore, and I probably wouldn't have liked it.  One caveat - the aluminum foil helps with cleanup, but I found as I tried to scrape every last bit of burnt cheese, it started to rip apart.  So, unless you want a little more metal in your diet, be careful of bits of foil in your spoon.  Great dish!

Flying Chicken Pa-Dak's menu includes common pizza, such as BBQ chicken & Margherita, along with fusion creations like bulgogi & sweet potato.  I'm a fan of Korean wings, and Flying Chicken Pa-Dak has wings in various ways - sweet garlic chicken, for example.  Their namesake, Pa-Dak, is chicken topped with green onions.

Service was good.  The wait wasn't very long & the attendant checked on me while having my lunch.  A fair amount of booth & table seating, with 2 flatscreen TV's & Korean pop on the speakers for entertainment.

Parking is in a private lot, shared by Caf√© Maji & the soon to be open Bruster's Real Ice Cream.

You have Pa-Dak to be kidding me!  You definitely have to check out Flying Chicken Pa-Dak, if you haven't already.  Have a slice of fusion pizza, some delicious Korean wings & a tipple or two of Sapporo or soju.  And, of course, don't forget about that corn cheese!  Just make sure to stay downwind of me after having it ;p

Highly recommend!
NOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOM</Review>< gmapID>

She indicated that she could not do anything for me except prescribe an antibiotic. I indicated I would probably have to go to an ER given the severity of the pain and the fact I couldn‚Äôt sleep to which she responded that we had to wait for the antibiotic to take hold.

She indicated that if it was not better to call back which I did after two days after which time it was much worse. Dr. Shiell then Saw me at a moments notice and provided treatment which relieved the swelling and subsequently the pain as well as change the antibiotic.

Upon return to have packing removed, PA Sharon seemed more concerned in making sure that the doctor had confirmed her diagnosis than in treating my wound.
The staff at West dermatology was first rate and the facilities are great as well. Dr. Shiell was better than good, he was very attentive, and followed through with good practice and professionalism. I believe Western Dermatology would benefit by replacing PA Sharon with someone who is a bit more professional and capable.
However, I would give West Dermatology 5 stars with the omission. Of the treatment by the PA.<//Review>

<date>1610737436978</date><rating>1</rating>< review>
I am so sad to say, I  will never shop here again over 3 wet bales of hay,  instead of just believing what a good customer was saying.  went on a camera that they have as people drive through,   said the bed of our truck was dry, and so was they hay.  It was stacked in our hay shed as soon as my husband got home, It had not rained for way over a week,  so when I opened one bale, it was wet all over the top of the bale, and had seeped into the hay, something you cannot feed horses.  I called and told them and one of the women gave me a credit for that bale and asked if there was anymore, which I had not checked,  so later found 2  more bales and not sure of the ones stacked on.  We were expected to drive back with the three bales if we wanted our money back.  there goes the gas, not to mention my poor husband of 65 would of had to lift up the bales into the truck, which is alot different then dropping them from a truck.  Anyway they lost a good  customer over three bales, because  they would not believe me, or just let me fax pictures.  It is quite a drive for us.  So Last batch was dusty and half looked like end bales, instead of the beautiful kentucky blue grass, which is 21 dollars a bale, so you expect the best.  and this batch, so far 3 wet bales.   Again lost a loyal customer, over three bales of hay</review>

It wasn't enough to justify a rhinoplasty for me, and I was worried about such major surgery and downtime.

<Review>While visiting my grandma in Central California, we decided to visit this beach, after coming here numerous times in the years prior. The beach is fantastic during low tide. It is notorious for containing multiple tide pools, as well as rocky beaches and rocks to climb. Wildlife as always is present, and you can get some fantastic pictures here. Parking and restrooms are, not a problem in this area, as they're both nearby. This is a fantastic place for pictures, as it provides interesting rock formations. If you can, climb up the big rock that's located on the north-western point of the beach, and you will get some fantastic shots of the scenery. Coming here during high-tide is not advised, as none of the things mentioned above are accessible due to the high water level. All in all, a great place to come especially if you're in the area.<//Review>< user>

Love this place. It's beautiful and peaceful. The walking trails along the bluffs offer wonderful views. The campground is basic with pit toilets and shorter parking pads at the sites which limits accessibility by larger RVs. There is a restored ranch house that offers tours and has a small nature store (no groceries). The aggressive racoons can be a problem.< /Review>
